table	process_scheduling_ed0395bf_3666_49e9_9db8_09fe997145b8	process_scheduling_ed0395bf_3666_49e9_9db8_09fe997145b8	0	CREATE VIRTUAL TABLE process_scheduling_ed0395bf_3666_49e9_9db8_09fe997145b8 USING __intrinsic_slice_mipmap((
        select
          s.id,
          s.ts,
          iif(
            s.dur = -1,
            ifnull(
              (
                select n.ts
                from tmp_ed0395bf_3666_49e9_9db8_09fe997145b8 n
                where n.ts > s.ts and n.cpu = s.cpu
                order by ts
                limit 1
              ),
              trace_end()
            ) - s.ts,
            s.dur
          ) as dur,
          s.cpu as depth
        from tmp_ed0395bf_3666_49e9_9db8_09fe997145b8 s
      ))
